"""Paged attention decode kernel for RTX 3090 (SM86).

Two-pass FlashDecoding-style Triton kernel:
  1. Each (batch, kv-head, chunk) block streams its KV pages and produces an
     unnormalized partial attention accumulator per query head in the GQA group.
  2. A tiny reduction kernel merges the per-chunk partials with the standard
     online-softmax combine rule and writes the final bf16 output.

This keeps all attention math in fp32 and only casts the final result back to
bf16, matching the reference numerics.
"""
import math

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import triton
import triton.language as tl

OP_TYPE = "attention"
SUPPORTED_PRECISIONS = ["bf16"]
HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_3090"]

# chunk size must be a multiple of PAGE_SIZE so token-to-page math stays simple
CHUNK_TOKENS = 64


@triton.autotune(
    configs=[
        triton.Config({}, num_warps=1),
        triton.Config({}, num_warps=2),
        triton.Config({}, num_warps=4),
        triton.Config({}, num_warps=8),
    ],
    key=["HEAD_DIM", "GROUP_SIZE"],
)
@triton.jit
def _paged_decode_partial(
    q_ptr,
    kv_cache_ptr,
    block_table_ptr,
    seq_lens_ptr,
    partial_o_ptr,
    partial_l_ptr,
    partial_m_ptr,
    scale,
    q_bstride,
    q_hstride,
    q_dstride,
    kv_nstride,
    kv_pstride,
    kv_hstride,
    kv_dstride,
    bt_bstride,
    bt_pstride,
    o_bstride,
    o_hstride,
    o_cstride,
    o_dstride,
    l_bstride,
    l_hstride,
    l_cstride,
    m_bstride,
    m_hstride,
    m_cstride,
    HEAD_DIM: tl.constexpr,
    GROUP_SIZE: tl.constexpr,
    PAGE_SIZE: tl.constexpr,
    CHUNK: tl.constexpr,
):
    """Compute partial attention for one (batch, kv-head, chunk)."""
    pid_c = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_hkv = tl.program_id(1)
    pid_b = tl.program_id(2)

    seq_len_b = tl.load(seq_lens_ptr + pid_b)
    chunk_start = pid_c * CHUNK
    if chunk_start >= seq_len_b:
        return

    # Load the G query heads belonging to this KV head.
    q_offs_g = tl.arange(0, GROUP_SIZE)[:, None]
    q_offs_d = tl.arange(0, HEAD_DIM)[None, :]
    q_head0 = pid_hkv * GROUP_SIZE
    q_ptrs = (
        q_ptr
        + pid_b * q_bstride
        + (q_head0 + q_offs_g) * q_hstride
        + q_offs_d * q_dstride
    )
    q = tl.load(q_ptrs).to(tl.float32)

    # Online softmax state (one scalar per query head).
    m = tl.full((GROUP_SIZE,), float("-inf"), dtype=tl.float32)
    denom = tl.zeros((GROUP_SIZE,), dtype=tl.float32)
    out = tl.zeros((GROUP_SIZE, HEAD_DIM), dtype=tl.float32)

    pages_per_chunk = CHUNK // PAGE_SIZE
    base_page = pid_c * pages_per_chunk
    physical_block = tl.cast(0, tl.int64)

    # Iterate over the fixed-size chunk; pages change every PAGE_SIZE tokens.
    for t in tl.static_range(0, CHUNK):
        global_token = chunk_start + t
        valid = global_token < seq_len_b

        if valid:
            if t % PAGE_SIZE == 0:
                page_idx = base_page + (t // PAGE_SIZE)
                physical_block = tl.load(
                    block_table_ptr + pid_b * bt_bstride + page_idx * bt_pstride
                ).to(tl.int64)

            offset = t % PAGE_SIZE
            kv_base = (
                kv_cache_ptr
                + physical_block * kv_nstride
                + offset * kv_pstride
                + pid_hkv * kv_hstride
            )
            kv_vec = tl.load(
                kv_base + tl.arange(0, 2 * HEAD_DIM) * kv_dstride
            ).to(tl.float32)
            k, v = tl.split(tl.reshape(kv_vec, (2, HEAD_DIM)).T)
            scores = tl.sum(q * k[None, :], axis=1) * scale
            masked_scores = scores
        else:
            masked_scores = tl.full((GROUP_SIZE,), float("-inf"), dtype=tl.float32)
            v = tl.zeros((HEAD_DIM,), dtype=tl.float32)

        # Online softmax update.
        new_m = tl.maximum(m, masked_scores)
        exp_old = tl.exp(m - new_m)
        exp_s = tl.exp(masked_scores - new_m)
        denom = denom * exp_old + exp_s
        out = out * exp_old[:, None] + v[None, :] * exp_s[:, None]
        m = new_m

    # Write unnormalized partials for every query head in the group.
    o_ptrs = partial_o_ptr + pid_b * o_bstride + (q_head0 + q_offs_g) * o_hstride
    o_ptrs = o_ptrs + pid_c * o_cstride + tl.arange(0, HEAD_DIM)[None, :] * o_dstride
    tl.store(o_ptrs, out)

    l_ptrs = partial_l_ptr + pid_b * l_bstride + (q_head0 + tl.arange(0, GROUP_SIZE)) * l_hstride + pid_c * l_cstride
    tl.store(l_ptrs, denom)

    m_ptrs = partial_m_ptr + pid_b * m_bstride + (q_head0 + tl.arange(0, GROUP_SIZE)) * m_hstride + pid_c * m_cstride
    tl.store(m_ptrs, m)


@triton.jit
def _paged_decode_reduce(
    partial_o_ptr,
    partial_l_ptr,
    partial_m_ptr,
    out_ptr,
    num_chunks,
    o_bstride,
    o_hstride,
    o_cstride,
    o_dstride,
    l_bstride,
    l_hstride,
    l_cstride,
    m_bstride,
    m_hstride,
    m_cstride,
    out_bstride,
    out_hstride,
    out_dstride,
    HEAD_DIM: tl.constexpr,
):
    """Merge per-chunk partials into the final attention output."""
    pid_h = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_b = tl.program_id(1)

    acc_m = tl.full((), float("-inf"), dtype=tl.float32)
    acc_l = tl.zeros((), dtype=tl.float32)
    acc_o = tl.zeros((HEAD_DIM,), dtype=tl.float32)

    for c in range(num_chunks):
        m_c = tl.load(partial_m_ptr + pid_b * m_bstride + pid_h * m_hstride + c * m_cstride)
        l_c = tl.load(partial_l_ptr + pid_b * l_bstride + pid_h * l_hstride + c * l_cstride)
        o_c = tl.load(
            partial_o_ptr
            + pid_b * o_bstride
            + pid_h * o_hstride
            + c * o_cstride
            + tl.arange(0, HEAD_DIM) * o_dstride
        )

        new_m = tl.maximum(acc_m, m_c)
        exp_acc = tl.exp(acc_m - new_m)
        exp_c = tl.exp(m_c - new_m)
        acc_l = acc_l * exp_acc + l_c * exp_c
        acc_o = acc_o * exp_acc + o_c * exp_c
        acc_m = new_m

    acc_o = acc_o / acc_l

    tl.store(
        out_ptr + pid_b * out_bstride + pid_h * out_hstride + tl.arange(0, HEAD_DIM) * out_dstride,
        acc_o.to(out_ptr.dtype.element_ty),
    )


class Model(nn.Module):
    """Single-query paged attention decode with a custom Triton kernel."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        batch: int,
        num_heads: int,
        num_kv_heads: int,
        head_dim: int,
        seq_len: int,
        page_size: int,
    ):
        super().__init__()
        assert num_heads % num_kv_heads == 0
        self.batch = batch
        self.num_heads = num_heads
        self.num_kv_heads = num_kv_heads
        self.head_dim = head_dim
        self.seq_len = seq_len
        self.page_size = page_size
        self.group_size = num_heads // num_kv_heads
        self.scale = 1.0 / math.sqrt(head_dim)

        self.register_buffer("_dummy", torch.zeros(1, dtype=torch.bfloat16), persistent=False)

    def forward(
        self,
        query: torch.Tensor,
        kv_cache: torch.Tensor,
        block_table: torch.Tensor,
        seq_lens: torch.Tensor,
    ) -> torch.Tensor:
        B, H, D = query.shape
        Hkv = self.num_kv_heads
        G = self.group_size
        P = self.page_size
        L = int(seq_lens.max().item()) if seq_lens.numel() else self.seq_len

        num_chunks = triton.cdiv(L, CHUNK_TOKENS)

        partial_o = torch.empty(B, H, num_chunks, D, dtype=torch.float32, device=query.device)
        partial_l = torch.empty(B, H, num_chunks, dtype=torch.float32, device=query.device)
        partial_m = torch.empty(B, H, num_chunks, dtype=torch.float32, device=query.device)

        grid_partial = (num_chunks, Hkv, B)
        _paged_decode_partial[grid_partial](
            query,
            kv_cache,
            block_table,
            seq_lens,
            partial_o,
            partial_l,
            partial_m,
            self.scale,
            query.stride(0),
            query.stride(1),
            query.stride(2),
            kv_cache.stride(0),
            kv_cache.stride(1),
            kv_cache.stride(2),
            kv_cache.stride(3),
            block_table.stride(0),
            block_table.stride(1),
            partial_o.stride(0),
            partial_o.stride(1),
            partial_o.stride(2),
            partial_o.stride(3),
            partial_l.stride(0),
            partial_l.stride(1),
            partial_l.stride(2),
            partial_m.stride(0),
            partial_m.stride(1),
            partial_m.stride(2),
            HEAD_DIM=D,
            GROUP_SIZE=G,
            PAGE_SIZE=P,
            CHUNK=CHUNK_TOKENS,
        )

        out = torch.empty(B, H, D, dtype=query.dtype, device=query.device)
        grid_reduce = (H, B)
        _paged_decode_reduce[grid_reduce](
            partial_o,
            partial_l,
            partial_m,
            out,
            num_chunks,
            partial_o.stride(0),
            partial_o.stride(1),
            partial_o.stride(2),
            partial_o.stride(3),
            partial_l.stride(0),
            partial_l.stride(1),
            partial_l.stride(2),
            partial_m.stride(0),
            partial_m.stride(1),
            partial_m.stride(2),
            out.stride(0),
            out.stride(1),
            out.stride(2),
            HEAD_DIM=D,
            num_warps=4,
        )

        return out


def get_inputs() -> list[torch.Tensor]:
    """Build random paged inputs for the current module-level shape knobs."""
    from reference import BATCH, HEAD_DIM, NUM_HEADS, NUM_KV_HEADS, PAGE_SIZE, SEQ_LEN

    B = BATCH
    H = NUM_HEADS
    Hkv = NUM_KV_HEADS
    D = HEAD_DIM
    L = SEQ_LEN
    P = PAGE_SIZE

    pages_per_seq = (L + P - 1) // P
    total_pages = max(B * pages_per_seq + 8, 64)

    query = torch.randn(B, H, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
    kv_cache = torch.randn(total_pages, P, Hkv, 2 * D, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1

    perm = torch.randperm(total_pages)[: B * pages_per_seq].reshape(B, pages_per_seq).int()
    block_table = perm.contiguous()
    seq_lens = torch.full((B,), L, dtype=torch.int32)

    return [query, kv_cache, block_table, seq_lens]


def get_init_inputs() -> list[int]:
    from reference import BATCH, HEAD_DIM, NUM_HEADS, NUM_KV_HEADS, PAGE_SIZE, SEQ_LEN
    return [BATCH, NUM_HEADS, NUM_KV_HEADS, HEAD_DIM, SEQ_LEN, PAGE_SIZE]
Done. `solution.py` in the current workspace now contains a custom Triton FlashDecoding-style paged-attention decode kernel for SM86/RTX 3090. What it does: - Two kernels: a partial kernel over `(batch, kv-head, chunk)` that streams pages, and a reduction kernel that merges per-chunk partials with online softmax. - Groups query heads by KV head so each KV page is read once per GQA group. - Loads the packed `[K|V]` vector as a single contiguous load and splits it with `tl.split`. - All attention math is fp32; only the final output is cast back to bf16. - Handles non-power-of-2 `seq_len` and predicated tails. 1	"""Naive PyTorch paged-attention decode reference (correctness oracle, not SOTA).
2	
3	Single-query decode: each batch element has a query of shape (num_heads, head_dim)
4	and attends over a KV cache of `seq_len[b]` tokens stored as fixed-size pages in
5	a global pool. Pages for batch element b are listed in `block_table[b]`.
6	
7	The reference performs the slow path:
8	  1. Gather pages -> contiguous (seq_len, num_kv_heads, head_dim) per batch element.
9	  2. Repeat KV heads for grouped-query (broadcast num_kv_heads -> num_heads).
10	  3. Manual softmax(QK^T / sqrt(d)) @ V in fp32, cast back to bf16.
11	
12	This avoids torch.nn.functional.scaled_dot_product_attention (which is on the
13	forbidden list) so the agent cannot dispatch through SDPA either.
14	"""
15	import math
16	
17	import torch
18	import torch.nn as nn
19	
20	OP_TYPE = "attention"
21	SUPPORTED_PRECISIONS = ["bf16"]
22	HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_PRO_6000", "H100", "B200"]
23	
24	
25	# --- Shape knobs (overridden by check.py / benchmark.py from shapes.py) ----
26	BATCH = 8
27	NUM_HEADS = 32
28	NUM_KV_HEADS = 8
29	HEAD_DIM = 128
30	SEQ_LEN = 1024
31	PAGE_SIZE = 16
32	
33	
34	class Model(nn.Module):
35	    """Single-query paged attention decode.
36	
37	    Forward inputs (all on device):
38	      query:       (batch, num_heads, head_dim)               bf16
39	      kv_cache:    (num_blocks, page_size, num_kv_heads, head_dim * 2)
40	                   Layout: last dim packs [K | V] so a single gather pulls both.

2	
3	Mix targets:
4	  - small batch / long context (Llama-3 8B-style decode)
5	  - large batch / medium context (server batched decode)
6	  - GQA wide ratio (Llama-3 70B: 64 heads / 8 kv-heads)
7	  - non-power-of-2 seq_len (forces predicated tail handling)
8	  - head_dim=64 small-head case
9	"""

Read /home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000517_kimi-claude_kimi-k2.7-code_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention/check.py

1	name: 03_paged_attention
2	display_name: "Paged Attention Decode"
3	precision: bf16
4	regime: memory  # decode is bandwidth-bound (KV cache streamed once per token)
5	
6	# Effective FLOPs per call: QK^T + softmax*V across all batches/heads/seq.
7	# Sum-formula evaluated per-shape; the benchmark substitutes batch/num_heads/etc.
8	# 2 * B * H * L * D for QK^T plus 2 * B * H * L * D for AV  =>  4 * B * H * L * D
9	flops_formula: "4 * batch * num_heads * seq_len * head_dim"
10	
11	# Bytes moved (the real bottleneck): the KV cache must be streamed end-to-end.
12	#   K and V each:  batch * seq_len * num_kv_heads * head_dim * 2 bytes (bf16)
13	#   Q: batch * num_heads * head_dim * 2  (negligible vs KV)
14	#   Out: same as Q
15	# So total ~ 2 * (B * L * Hkv * D * 2) + small.
16	bytes_formula: "2 * batch * seq_len * num_kv_heads * head_dim * 2 + batch * num_heads * head_dim * 2 * 2"
17	
18	hardware: [RTX_3090]
19	peak_tflops_key: bf16          # informational; regime=memory uses bandwidth
20	peak_bandwidth_key: dram        # 1.8 TB/s GDDR7 on RTX PRO 6000 Blackwell
21	
22	tolerance:
23	  bfloat16: 0.02
24	  float16: 0.02
25	
26	# Forbidden ops -- using any of these in solution.py fails correctness post-hoc.
27	# vllm.attention / flashinfer.batch_decode_with_paged_kv_cache: dispatching to
28	# the SOTA library is the trivial cheat. SDPA is also banned because the agent
29	# could gather pages then call SDPA and inherit FlashAttention "for free".
30	forbidden:
31	  - "vllm.attention"

+++ b//home/infatoshi/kernelbench.com/benchmarks/hard/outputs/runs/20260619_000517_kimi-claude_kimi-k2.7-code_03_paged_attention/repo/problems/03_paged_attention/solution.py

+"""Paged attention decode kernel for RTX 3090 (SM86).
+
+Two-pass FlashDecoding-style Triton kernel:
+  1. Each (batch, kv-head, chunk) block streams its KV pages and produces an
+     unnormalized partial attention accumulator per query head in the GQA group.
+  2. A tiny reduction kernel merges the per-chunk partials with the standard
+     online-softmax combine rule and writes the final bf16 output.
+
+This keeps all attention math in fp32 and only casts the final result back to
+bf16, matching the reference numerics.
+"""
+import math
+from typing import List
+
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+OP_TYPE = "attention"
+SUPPORTED_PRECISIONS = ["bf16"]
+HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_3090"]
+
+# chunk size must be a multiple of PAGE_SIZE so token-to-page math stays simple
+CHUNK_TOKENS = 128
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _paged_decode_partial(
+    q_ptr,
+    kv_cache_ptr,
+    block_table_ptr,
+    seq_lens_ptr,
+    partial_o_ptr,
+    partial_l_ptr,
+    partial_m_ptr,
+    scale,
+    q_bstride,
+    q_hstride,
+    q_dstride,
+    kv_nstride,
+    kv_pstride,
+    kv_hstride,
+    kv_dstride,
+    bt_bstride,
+    bt_pstride,
+    o_bstride,
+    o_hstride,
+    o_cstride,
+    o_dstride,
+    l_bstride,
+    l_hstride,
+    l_cstride,
+    m_bstride,
+    m_hstride,
+    m_cstride,
+    HEAD_DIM: tl.constexpr,
+    GROUP_SIZE: tl.constexpr,
+    PAGE_SIZE: tl.constexpr,
+    CHUNK: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    """Compute partial attention for one (batch, kv-head, chunk)."""
+    pid_c = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_hkv = tl.program_id(1)
+    pid_b = tl.program_id(2)
+
+    seq_len_b = tl.load(seq_lens_ptr + pid_b)
+    chunk_start = pid_c * CHUNK
+    chunk_end = chunk_start + CHUNK
+    if chunk_start >= seq_len_b:
+        return
+
+    # Load the G query heads belonging to this KV head.
+    q_offs_g = tl.arange(0, GROUP_SIZE)[:, None]
+    q_offs_d = tl.arange(0, HEAD_DIM)[None, :]
+    q_head0 = pid_hkv * GROUP_SIZE
+    q_ptrs = (
+        q_ptr
+        + pid_b * q_bstride
+        + (q_head0 + q_offs_g) * q_hstride
+        + q_offs_d * q_dstride
+    )
+    q = tl.load(q_ptrs).to(tl.float32)
+
+    # Online softmax state (one scalar per query head).
+    m = tl.full((GROUP_SIZE,), float("-inf"), dtype=tl.float32)
+    denom = tl.zeros((GROUP_SIZE,), dtype=tl.float32)
+    out = tl.zeros((GROUP_SIZE, HEAD_DIM), dtype=tl.float32)
+
+    pages_per_chunk = CHUNK // PAGE_SIZE
+    base_page = pid_c * pages_per_chunk
+    physical_block = tl.cast(0, tl.int64)
+
+    # Iterate over the fixed-size chunk; pages change every PAGE_SIZE tokens.
+    for t in tl.static_range(0, CHUNK):
+        global_token = chunk_start + t
+        if global_token >= seq_len_b:
+            break
+
+        if t % PAGE_SIZE == 0:
+            page_idx = base_page + (t // PAGE_SIZE)
+            physical_block = tl.load(
+                block_table_ptr + pid_b * bt_bstride + page_idx * bt_pstride
+            ).to(tl.int64)
+
+        offset = t % PAGE_SIZE
+        kv_base = (
+            kv_cache_ptr
+            + physical_block * kv_nstride
+            + offset * kv_pstride
+            + pid_hkv * kv_hstride
+        )
+        k = tl.load(kv_base + tl.arange(0, HEAD_DIM) * kv_dstride).to(tl.float32)
+        v = tl.load(
+            kv_base + (HEAD_DIM + tl.arange(0, HEAD_DIM)) * kv_dstride
+        ).to(tl.float32)
+
+        # Per-query-head scores for this token.
+        scores = tl.sum(q * k[None, :], axis=1) * scale
+
+        # Online softmax update.
+        new_m = tl.maximum(m, scores)
+        exp_old = tl.exp(m - new_m)
+        exp_s = tl.exp(scores - new_m)
+        denom = denom * exp_old + exp_s
+        out = out * exp_old[:, None] + v[None, :] * exp_s[:, None]
+        m = new_m
+
+    # Write unnormalized partials for every query head in the group.
+    o_ptrs = partial_o_ptr + pid_b * o_bstride + (q_head0 + q_offs_g) * o_hstride
+    o_ptrs = o_ptrs + pid_c * o_cstride + tl.arange(0, HEAD_DIM)[None, :] * o_dstride
+    tl.store(o_ptrs, out)
+
+    l_ptrs = partial_l_ptr + pid_b * l_bstride + (q_head0 + tl.arange(0, GROUP_SIZE)) * l_hstride + pid_c * l_cstride
+    tl.store(l_ptrs, denom)
+
+    m_ptrs = partial_m_ptr + pid_b * m_bstride + (q_head0 + tl.arange(0, GROUP_SIZE)) * m_hstride + pid_c * m_cstride
+    tl.store(m_ptrs, m)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _paged_decode_reduce(
+    partial_o_ptr,
+    partial_l_ptr,
+    partial_m_ptr,
+    out_ptr,
+    num_chunks,
+    o_bstride,
+    o_hstride,
+    o_cstride,
+    o_dstride,
+    l_bstride,
+    l_hstride,
+    l_cstride,
+    m_bstride,
+    m_hstride,
+    m_cstride,
+    out_bstride,
+    out_hstride,
+    out_dstride,
+    HEAD_DIM: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    """Merge per-chunk partials into the final attention output."""
+    pid_h = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_b = tl.program_id(1)
+
+    acc_m = tl.full((), float("-inf"), dtype=tl.float32)
+    acc_l = tl.zeros((), dtype=tl.float32)
+    acc_o = tl.zeros((HEAD_DIM,), dtype=tl.float32)
+
+    for c in range(num_chunks):
+        m_c = tl.load(partial_m_ptr + pid_b * m_bstride + pid_h * m_hstride + c * m_cstride)
+        l_c = tl.load(partial_l_ptr + pid_b * l_bstride + pid_h * l_hstride + c * l_cstride)
+        o_c = tl.load(
+            partial_o_ptr
+            + pid_b * o_bstride
+            + pid_h * o_hstride
+            + c * o_cstride
+            + tl.arange(0, HEAD_DIM) * o_dstride
+        )
+
+        new_m = tl.maximum(acc_m, m_c)
+        exp_acc = tl.exp(acc_m - new_m)
+        exp_c = tl.exp(m_c - new_m)
+        acc_l = acc_l * exp_acc + l_c * exp_c
+        acc_o = acc_o * exp_acc + o_c * exp_c
+        acc_m = new_m
+
+    acc_o = acc_o / acc_l
+
+    tl.store(
+        out_ptr + pid_b * out_bstride + pid_h * out_

... (4452 more chars)

reasoning (13515 chars)
Peak fraction geomean 0.1873. Not bad, but we can improve. The memory recollection says FlashDecoding Triton hits ~0.31. We are at 0.187. Need push number up. Shape 4 is low 0.083 (D=64, L=2000, B=8, H=16, Hkv=4). Others 0.17-0.27. Need optimize. What are bottlenecks? First kernel has per-token k/v load. Grouping reduces traffic. But we use two separate loads K and V. We might improve by loading D2 vector once. Also static loop of 128 with scalar if and physical_block load maybe causing divergence. The low fraction suggests bandwidth not fully utilized. We need profile with ncu. Use ncu or torch profiler. But first think. We can improve by: 1. Use tl.dot for Q*K to exploit tensor cores? But decode q length 1, not beneficial. Dot product could be faster with vector FMA? tl.sum(q*k) compiles to elementwise multiply + reduce. Might be okay. 2. Load K and V in one vector and split. Could halve load instructions and improve memory throughput. 3. Use block pointers or vectorized loads. Our loads are contiguous D elements per token, but all threads load same token. Wait, in Triton, loading `tl.arange(0,HEAD_DIM)` in a block with many threads means each thread loads a subset of elements (coalesced). That's fine. But because all threads need the same token vector, and q vector distributed across threads, the dot product requires reduction. Triton likely uses shared memory or shfl. Could be overhead. 4. Increase chunk size to reduce partial kernel overhead and increase per-block work? But chunk size must be multiple of page_size. CHUNK=128 gives enough chunks. Maybe larger chunk (256) reduces kernel launches and second reduction overhead. But also reduces parallelism for short L. Could autotune. 5. Use fewer warps? num_warps=8. For D=64, group_size=4, maybe 4 warps enough. For D=128,G=8, 8 warps. Could autotune. 6. Process multiple tokens per iteration to amortize physical_block loads and increase arithmetic intensity. For example, load a page (16 tokens) all at once as a tile of shape (PAGE_SIZE, D) and compute scores for all 16 tokens simultaneously. This would use more registers/shared memory but reduce loop overhead and allow vectorized loads across tokens. Similarly for V. However memory layout for a page: (page_size, head_dim) contiguous for K then V? The KV cache last dim packs [K|V] per token. A page's K tokens are stored as (page_size, D) contiguous? Actually kv_cache shape (num_blocks, page_size, Hkv, 2*D). For a given block and head, the token offsets dimension page_size is second, then 2*D last. +import torch
+import reference, shapes, solution
+
+# profile shape 0
+d = shapes.SHAPES[0]
+for k, v in d.items():
+    setattr(reference, k.upper(), v)
+
+B, H, Hkv, D, L, P = reference.get_init_inputs()
+model = solution.Model(B, H, Hkv, D, L, P).cuda().eval()
+inputs = [x.cuda() for x in reference.get_inputs()]
+
+# warmup
+for _ in range(5):
+    model(*inputs)
+torch.cuda.synchronize()
+
+# steady loop
+for _ in range(30):
+    out = model(*inputs)
+torch.cuda.synchronize()
+print("done", out.shape)

1	"""Paged attention decode kernel for RTX 3090 (SM86).
2	
3	Two-pass FlashDecoding-style Triton kernel:
4	  1. Each (batch, kv-head, chunk) block streams its KV pages and produces an
5	     unnormalized partial attention accumulator per query head in the GQA group.
6	  2. A tiny reduction kernel merges the per-chunk partials with the standard
7	     online-softmax combine rule and writes the final bf16 output.
8	
9	This keeps all attention math in fp32 and only casts the final result back to
10	bf16, matching the reference numerics.
11	"""
12	import math
13	from typing import List
14	
15	import torch
16	import torch.nn as nn
17	import triton
18	import triton.language as tl
19	
20	OP_TYPE = "attention"
21	SUPPORTED_PRECISIONS = ["bf16"]
22	HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_3090"]
23	
24	# chunk size must be a multiple of PAGE_SIZE so token-to-page math stays simple
25	CHUNK_TOKENS = 96
26	
27

30	        triton.Config({}, num_warps=2),

1	"""Paged attention decode kernel for RTX 3090 (SM86).
2	
3	Two-pass FlashDecoding-style Triton kernel:
4	  1. Each (batch, kv-head, chunk) block streams its KV pages and produces an
5	     unnormalized partial attention accumulator per query head in the GQA group.
6	  2. A tiny reduction kernel merges the per-chunk partials with the standard
7	     online-softmax combine rule and writes the final bf16 output.
8	
9	This keeps all attention math in fp32 and only casts the final result back to
10	bf16, matching the reference numerics.
11	"""
12	import math
13	
14	import torch
15	import torch.nn as nn
16	import triton
17	import triton.language as tl
18	
19	OP_TYPE = "attention"
20	SUPPORTED_PRECISIONS = ["bf16"]
21	HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_3090"]
22	
23	# chunk size must be a multiple of PAGE_SIZE so token-to-page math stays simple
24	CHUNK_TOKENS = 64
25	
26	
27	@triton.autotune(
28	    configs=[
29	        triton.Config({}, num_warps=1),
30	        triton.Config({}, num_warps=2),
31	        triton.Config({}, num_warps=4),
32	        triton.Config({}, num_warps=8),
33	    ],
34	    key=["HEAD_DIM", "GROUP_SIZE"],
35	)
36	@triton.jit
37	def _paged_decode_partial(
38	    q_ptr,
39	    kv_cache_ptr,
40	    block_table_ptr,
41	    seq_lens_ptr,
42	    partial_o_ptr,
43	    partial_l_ptr,
44	    partial_m_ptr,
45	    scale,
46	    q_bstride,
47	    q_hstride,
48	    q_dstride,
49	    kv_nstride,
50	    kv_pstride,
51	    kv_hstride,
52	    kv_dstride,
53	    bt_bstride,
54	    bt_

assistant
Done. `solution.py` in the current workspace now contains a custom Triton FlashDecoding-style paged-attention decode kernel for SM86/RTX 3090. What it does: - Two kernels: a partial kernel over `(batch, kv-head, chunk)` that streams pages, and a reduction kernel that merges per-chunk partials with online softmax. - Groups query heads by KV head so each KV page is read once per GQA group. - Loads the packed `[K|V]` vector as a single contiguous load and splits it with `tl.split`. - All attention math is fp32; only the final output is cast back to bf16. - Handles non-power-of-2 `seq_len` and predicated tails. Verification: - `uv run python check.py` → **PASS** across all five shapes and all seeds. - `uv run ruff check problems/03_paged_attention/solution.py` → **All checks passed**. - No forbidden ops in `solution.py`. Benchmark (`uv run python benchmark.py`): - shape 0 (8/32/8/128/1024): 0.328 peak fraction - shape 1 (32/32/8/128/2048): 0.663 - shape 2 (4/64/8/128/4096): 0.364 - shape 3 (16/32/8/128/1535): 0.506 - shape 4 (8/16/4/64/2000): 0.191 - geomean peak fraction: **0.377** → RESULT: OK I removed the temporary `profile.py` scratch file; the only final artifact is `solution.py`.
